<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  // Get current URL and parse it
  var currentUrl = window.location.href;
  var parser = new URL(currentUrl);

  // Extract the source path for MPC_3
  var sourcePath = parser.pathname;

  // Get the value of MPC_1 from the current URL for MPC_4
  var currentParams = new URLSearchParams(parser.search);
  var currentMPC_1 = currentParams.get('MPC_1');

  // Array of sitelink attribute values to target
  var sitelinkValues = [
    "Recommended",
    "Art-Popular",
		"Home-First",
		"Home-Top",
    "Home-Recommended",
    "Home-Spacial",
    "Home-Bottom",
    "Category-top",
    "Category-News",
    "Category-Popular"
  ];

  sitelinkValues.forEach(function(sitelinkValue) {
    // Find all divs with the current sitelink attribute value
    var divs = document.querySelectorAll('div[sitelink="' + sitelinkValue + '"]');

    divs.forEach(function(div) {
      // Find all links within the div
      var links = div.querySelectorAll('a[href]');

      links.forEach(function(link) {
        var linkHref = link.getAttribute('href');
        var linkUrl = new URL(linkHref, window.location.origin);

        // Build new query parameters
        var params = new URLSearchParams(linkUrl.search);

        params.set('MPC_1', 'Haiton11');
        params.set('MPC_2', sitelinkValue); // Use the sitelink value for MPC_2
        params.set('MPC_3', sourcePath);

        if (currentMPC_1) {
          params.set('MPC_4', currentMPC_1);
        }

        // Update the link's href attribute with new parameters
        linkUrl.search = params.toString();
        link.setAttribute('href', linkUrl.toString());
      });
    });
  });
});
</script>

<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 5: Elementor form phone validation -->
<script>
(function($) {
    $(document).ready(function() {
        // Fields
        var nameField = $('#form-field-fullname');
        var emailField = $('#form-field-email');
        var phoneField = $('#form-field-phone');
        var submitButton = $('#submit');

        // If the phone field doesn't exist, exit the script early.
        if (!phoneField.length) {
            return;
        }

        var hasUserInputStarted = false;
        var initialBorderStyle = phoneField.css('border');

        // Disable submit button, reduce opacity, and add a red border if phone field value doesn't meet criteria.
        function updateSubmitButton() {
            var phoneValue = phoneField.val();
            var isValidPhone = phoneValue.length === 10 && phoneValue.startsWith('05') && /^\d+$/.test(phoneValue);

            if (hasUserInputStarted) {
                submitButton.prop('disabled', !isValidPhone).css('opacity', isValidPhone ? 1 : 0.5);
                phoneField.css('border', isValidPhone ? initialBorderStyle : '1px solid red');
            }
        }

        phoneField.on('input', function() {
            var newValue = phoneField.val().replace(/\D/g, '');
            phoneField.val(newValue);
            hasUserInputStarted = true;
            updateSubmitButton();
        });

        updateSubmitButton();

        // Custom error message function
				function addCustomErrorMessage(field, message) {
						if (field.length === 0) {
								console.warn('Field not found:', field.selector);
								return;
						}

						field.get(0).addEventListener('invalid', function(event) {
								event.target.setCustomValidity('');
								if (!event.target.validity.valid) {
										event.target.setCustomValidity(message);
								}
						});

    field.get(0).addEventListener('input', function(event) {
        event.target.setCustomValidity('');
    });
}


        // Add custom error messages
        addCustomErrorMessage(nameField, 'נא להזין שם מלא תקין');
        addCustomErrorMessage(emailField, 'נא להזין אימייל תקין');
        addCustomErrorMessage(phoneField, 'נא להזין מספר טלפון נייד תקין');
    });
})(jQuery);
</script>

<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->
<!-- HFCM by 99 Robots - Snippet # 9: Redirect Parameters V3 with pixelId (Page Wide) -->
<script>
(function() {
    function updateAnchorLinks(queryParams) {
        var matches = document.querySelectorAll(".link-param a");

        // Get the current page URL (excluding query parameters)
        var currentPageUrl = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname;

        // Alternatively, include query parameters by using:
        // var currentPageUrl = window.location.href;

        // Add the referrer parameter
        queryParams.set('referrer', currentPageUrl);

        matches.forEach(element => {
            var url = new URL(element.href);

            // Append all the search params from queryParams to the anchor element
            for (const [key, value] of queryParams.entries()) {
                url.searchParams.set(key, value);
            }

            element.href = url.toString();
        });
    }

    function initialLinkUpdate() {
        var queryString = window.location.search;
        var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(queryString);

        // Call updateAnchorLinks with current URL parameters
        updateAnchorLinks(urlParams);
    }

    function updateLinksWithPixelId(pixelId) {
        var queryString = window.location.search;
        var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(queryString);

        // Add the pixelId to the query parameters
        urlParams.set('pixelId', pixelId);

        // Call updateAnchorLinks with updated parameters
        updateAnchorLinks(urlParams);
    }

    function waitForPixelId(attempts) {
        attempts = attempts || 0;
        var maxAttempts = 20; // Maximum number of attempts
        var delay = 500; // Delay between attempts in milliseconds

        function getPixelId() {
            if (typeof fbq === 'function' && fbq.getState) {
                var pixelState = fbq.getState();
                if (pixelState && pixelState.pixels && pixelState.pixels[0] && pixelState.pixels[0].id) {
                    return pixelState.pixels[0].id;
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        var pixelId = getPixelId();

        if (pixelId) {
            updateLinksWithPixelId(pixelId);
            console.log('Links updated with pixelId:', pixelId);
        } else {
            if (attempts < maxAttempts) {
                console.log('pixelId not available yet. Attempt:', attempts + 1);
                setTimeout(function() {
                    waitForPixelId(attempts + 1);
                }, delay);
            } else {
                console.log('Max attempts reached. pixelId is still not available.');
            }
        }
    }

    // Run the initial link update after the DOM content is loaded
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        initialLinkUpdate();
        waitForPixelId();
    });
})();
</script>

<!-- /end HFCM by 99 Robots -->
			<script>
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function() {
    function setPixelIdToUtmIdField(attempts) {
        attempts = attempts || 0;
        var maxAttempts = 20; // Adjust as needed
        var delay = 500; // Delay between attempts in milliseconds
        try {
            // Check if fbq is defined
            if (typeof fbq === 'function' && fbq.getState) {
                var pixelState = fbq.getState();
                console.log('fbq.getState():', pixelState);
                if (pixelState && pixelState.pixels && pixelState.pixels[0] && pixelState.pixels[0].id) {
                    var pixelId = pixelState.pixels[0].id;
                    console.log('Pixel ID found after', attempts, 'attempt(s):', pixelId);
                    // Find all inputs with name 'form_fields[utm_id]'
                    var inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="form_fields[utm_id]"]');
                    inputs.forEach(function(input) {
                        // Set the value to the pixelId
                        input.value = pixelId;
                        console.log('Set pixelId value in utm_id input:', input);
                    });
                } else {
                    console.log('Pixel ID not found in fbq.getState().');
                }
            } else {
                if (attempts < maxAttempts) {
//                     console.log('fbq is not defined yet. Attempt:', attempts + 1);
                    // Try again after a short delay
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        setPixelIdToUtmIdField(attempts + 1);
                    }, delay);
                } else {
                    console.log('Max attempts reached. fbq is still not defined.');
                }
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error('Error setting pixelId value:', e);
        }
    }
    // Start the function after the DOM is loaded
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        setPixelIdToUtmIdField();
    });
})();
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
(function() {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Function to get query parameter by name
        function getQueryParam(name) {
            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            return urlParams.get(name);
        }
        
        // Function to get cookie by name
        function getCookie(name) {
            var value = "; " + document.cookie;
            var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
            if (parts.length === 2) {
                return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
            }
            return null;
        }
        
        // Get the fbclid parameter from the URL
        var fbclid = getQueryParam('fbclid');
        if (fbclid) {
            // Find all inputs with name 'form_fields[MPC_5]'
            var inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="form_fields[MPC_5]"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(function(input) {
                    input.value = fbclid;
                    console.log('Set fbclid value in MPC_5 input:', input);
                });
            } else {
                console.log('MPC_5 input not found in the form.');
            }
        } else {
            console.log('fbclid not found in URL.');
        }
        
        // Get the _fbp cookie
        var fbp = getCookie('_fbp');
        if (fbp) {
            // Find all inputs with name 'form_fields[MPC_38]'
            var fbpInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="form_fields[MPC_38]"]');
            if (fbpInputs.length > 0) {
                fbpInputs.forEach(function(input) {
                    input.value = fbp;
                    console.log('Set _fbp value in MPC_38 input:', input);
                });
            } else {
                console.log('MPC_38 input not found in the form.');
            }
        } else {
            console.log('_fbp cookie not found.');
        }
    });
})();
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
  (function () {
   function updateLinksWithField(fieldName, value) {
      console.log(
         "[addIpAndUserAgent] |  updateLinksWithField | fieldName: ",
         fieldName,
         " | value: ",
         value
      );

      // get all url's (a tags and buttons)
      document.querySelectorAll("a, button").forEach((element) => {
         // get the url property.
         let url = element.tagName === "A" ? element.href : element.getAttribute("data-url");

         // check if its going to form
         if (url && url.includes("-form")) {
            console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] |  updateLinksWithField | Found URL: ", url);

            let urlObj = new URL(url);
            let params = new URLSearchParams(urlObj.search);

            // only when it's not already added.
            if (!params.has(fieldName)) {
               // update the url params
               params.append(fieldName, value);
               urlObj.search = params.toString();

               // update the element url property
               if (element.tagName === "A") {
                  element.href = urlObj.toString();
               } else if (element.tagName === "BUTTON") {
                  element.setAttribute("data-url", urlObj.toString());
               }

               console.log(
                  "[addIpAndUserAgent] |  updateLinksWithField | Updated URL: ",
                  urlObj.toString()
               );
            }
         }
      });
   }

   // Helper function to populate all fields by name across all forms
   function populateAllFieldsByName(fieldName, value) {
      console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] | populateAllFieldsByName => fieldName: ", fieldName);
      const fields = document.querySelectorAll(`[name="form_fields[${fieldName}]"]`);
      console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] | populateAllFieldsByName => fields: ", fields);
      if (fields.length > 0) {
         fields.forEach((field) => {
            field.value = value;
            console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] | populateAllFieldsByName => field: ", field);
            // Trigger change event to ensure Elementor recognizes the update
            const event = new Event("input", { bubbles: true });
            field.dispatchEvent(event);
         });
      } else {
         console.log("Field not found: ", fieldName);
      }
   }

   // Use the IP from WordPress instead of an external API
   if (window.USER_IP) {
      console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] | USER_IP (from WP): ", window.USER_IP);
      populateAllFieldsByName("ip", window.USER_IP);
      updateLinksWithField("ip", window.USER_IP);
   } else {
      console.warn("[addIpAndUserAgent] | USER_IP not available from WordPress.");
      // Fetch the user's IP address using a third-party API
      fetch("https://api.ipify.org?format=json")
         .then((response) => response.json())
         .then((data) => {
            // Populate the 'ip' field with the user's IP address
            console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] | user ip: ", data.ip);
            populateAllFieldsByName("ip", data.ip);
            updateLinksWithField("ip", data.ip);
         })
         .catch((error) => console.error("Error fetching IP address:", error));
   }

   // Get the user's User-Agent and populate the 'agent' field
   console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] | user agent: ", navigator.userAgent);
   populateAllFieldsByName("agent", navigator.userAgent);
   updateLinksWithField("agent", navigator.userAgent);
   // Get the current page URL and populate the 'page-url' field
   const currentPageUrl = window.location.href;
   console.log("[addIpAndUserAgent] |currentPageUrl: ", currentPageUrl);
   populateAllFieldsByName("page-url", currentPageUrl);
//    updateLinksWithField("page-url", currentPageUrl);
   populateAllFieldsByName("page_url", currentPageUrl);
//    updateLinksWithField("page_url", currentPageUrl);
   populateAllFieldsByName("page", currentPageUrl);
//    updateLinksWithField("page", currentPageUrl);
})();
</script>
